<script>
		$(function(){
			$('.SearchWrap .SummonerName').on('focus', function(){
				$(window).scrollTop($(this).closest('.SearchWrap').offset().top - 16);
				$('.auto-complete').show();
			});

			var $titleAction = $(".auto-complete__title--action");
			var autoCompleteContentList = $titleAction.parent();
			autoCompleteContentList.eq(0).addClass("on");
			$titleAction.on("click", function(e){
				var $this = $(this);
				e.preventDefault();
				autoCompleteContentList.removeClass("on");
				$this.parent().addClass("on")
			});

			var $layoutMenu = $('.layout__menu');
			var $menu = $('.menu', $layoutMenu), isFixed = false;
			var isForum = location.pathname.indexOf('forum') !== -1 ? true : false;

			if(!isForum) {
                $(window).on('scroll', function(){
                    if($(this).scrollTop() > $layoutMenu.offset().top && !isFixed) {
                        $menu.addClass('menu--fixed');
                        isFixed = true;
                    }
                    if($(this).scrollTop() <= $layoutMenu.offset().top && isFixed) {
                        $menu.removeClass('menu--fixed');
                        isFixed = false;
                    }
                });
			}
		});
	</script>

<script>
$(document).ready(function () {
  $('#summoner-search-form').on('submit', function(e) {
    e.preventDefault();
    var $this = $(this);
    var username = $this.find('#searchUserName').val();

    window.location.href = $this.attr('action') + 'userName=' + username;
  });

  (function () { // tab test
    $tab = $('[class^="c-tab__"]'),
    $tabItem = $tab.find('[class*="item"]');
    $tabItem.on('click', function () {
      var _this = $(this);
      className = _this[0].classList[0],
      activeClass = className + '--is-active';
      _this.addClass(activeClass).siblings().removeClass(activeClass);
    });

    // Hide layer-dim self
    /* var $layerDim = $(".layer-dim");
      $layerDim.click(function () {
        $layerDim.hide();
      }) */
  })();

  (function () {
    var $opggNav = $('.opgg-header__navi-box'),
      $btnNaviOpen = $('.opgg-header__navi-open'),
      $btnNaviClose = $('.opgg-header__navi-close'),
      openClass = 'opgg-header__navi-box--is-open';

    $btnNaviOpen.on('click', function () {
      $opggNav.toggleClass(openClass);
    })
    $btnNaviClose.on('click', function () {
      $opggNav.removeClass(openClass);
    })
  })();

  (function () {
    var $opggUtil = $('.opgg-header__util-box'),
      $btnUtilOpen = $('.opgg-header__util-open'),
      $btnUtilClose = $('.opgg-header__util-close'),
      openClass = 'opgg-header__util-box--is-open';

    $btnUtilOpen.on('click', function () {
      $opggUtil.toggleClass(openClass);
    })
    $btnUtilClose.on('click', function () {
      $opggUtil.removeClass(openClass);
    })
  })();

});
</script>

<script>
	// 임시 스크립트
	var confirmForcePC = function(obj){
		var isShowMessage = $(obj).data('isShowMessage');
		if (isShowMessage == '1') {
			$(obj).data('isShowMessage', '0');
			Tipped.get(obj).remove();
		} else {
			$(obj).data('isShowMessage', '1');
			var message = "이 메뉴는 PC 버전만 볼 수 있습니다. 한번 더 터치해주세요.";
			var tp = Tipped.create(obj, message, {
				radius: false,
				maxWidth: 320,
				position: 'bottomLeft',
				fadeIn: 0,
				fadeOut: 0
			}).show();
			return false;
		}
	};
</script>

    (function () {
        var headerButton = document.querySelector(".opscore-banner__header--button");
        var headerButtonIcon = document.querySelector(".opscore-banner__header--button-icon");
        var content = document.querySelector(".opscore-banner__content");
        var footer = document.querySelector(".opscore-banner__footer");
        var spinClassName = "opscore-banner__header--button-icon-spin";

        headerButton.onclick = function () {
            headerButtonIcon.classList.toggle(spinClassName);
            content.classList.toggle("hide");
            footer.classList.toggle("hide");

<script>
  (function () {
    var miniBanner = document.querySelector(".app--install--mini--container");
    document.getElementById("appInstallMiniCloseIcon").addEventListener("click", hideBanner);
    function hideBanner() {
      miniBanner.style.display = "none";
      if (!$.cookie("closedMobileAppInstallMini")) {

        $.cookie("closedMobileAppInstallMini", "true", {
          path: "/",
          expires: 9999
        });
      }
      event.stopPropagation();
    }
    window.onload = function () {
      if (!$.cookie("closedMobileAppInstallMini")) {
        miniBanner.className += " animation";
      }
    }
  })()
</script> <div class="mobile-app-install">

<script>
  (function () {
    var banner = document.querySelector(".mobile-app-install");
    document.getElementById("appInstallCloseButton").addEventListener("click", function () {
      if (!$.cookie("closedMobileAppInstall")) {
        banner.style.display = "none";
        $.cookie("closedMobileAppInstall", "true", {
          path: "/",
          expires: 9999
        });
        document.querySelector(".app--install--mini--container").className += " animation";
      }
    });
    window.onload = function () {
      if (!$.cookie("closedMobileAppInstall")) {
        banner.className += " animation";
      } else if (!$.cookie("closedMobileAppInstallMini")) {
        document.querySelector(".app--install--mini--container").className += " animation";
      }
    }
  })()

<script>
		window.lifeOnwer = function(){
			this.randAdIdx = '1864751992';
			this.showAd = function(element, size){
				if (size === "skyscraper") {
					this.showAdSkyscraper();
					return;
				}
				element.innerHTML = this.getAdHTML(size);
				element.classList.remove('vm-placement');
			};

			this.showAdSkyscraper = function(){
				if (this.getMobileOS() !== "unknown") {
					return;
				}

				var elementLeft = document.createElement("div");
				elementLeft.innerHTML = this.getAdHTML("skyscraper");
				elementLeft.setAttribute('style', 'position: absolute; left: 50%; top: 106px; margin-left: -725px;');
				document.body.appendChild(elementLeft);

				var elementRight = document.createElement("div");
				elementRight.innerHTML = this.getAdHTML("skyscraper");
				elementRight.setAttribute('style', 'position: absolute; right: 50%; top: 106px; margin-right: -725px;');
				document.body.appendChild(elementRight);

				$(elementRight).scrollToFixed({
					marginTop: 60
				});
			};

			this.getAdHTML = function(size){
				var lang = (this.getLang() === 'ko_KR' ? 'ko' : 'en');
				return "<a href=\"" + this.getAdLink(this.adIndex) + "\" target=\"_blank\" class=\"lifeOnwer-" + randAdIdx + "\">" +
					"<img src='//opgg-static.akamaized.net/images/lifeowner/opgg/" + lang + "/" + adIndex + "-" + size + ".png'>" +
					"</a>";
			};
			this.getAdLink = function(adIndex){
				var linkKey = this.getMobileOS() + '-' + adIndex;
				switch (linkKey) {
					case "Android-1":
						return "market://details?id=gg.op.lol.android&referrer=utm_source%3Dopgg%26utm_medium%3Dbanner01%26utm_content%3Dapp";
					case "Android-2":
						return "market://details?id=gg.op.lol.android&referrer=utm_source%3Dopgg%26utm_medium%3Dbanner02%26utm_content%3Dlol";
					case "Android-3":
						return "market://details?id=gg.op.lol.android&referrer=utm_source%3Dopgg%26utm_medium%3banner03%26utm_content%3Dpubg";
					case "unknown-1":
						return "https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=gg.op.lol.android&referrer=utm_source%3Dopgg%26utm_medium%3Dbanner01%26utm_content%3Dapp";
					case "unknown-2":
						return "https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=gg.op.lol.android&referrer=utm_source%3Dopgg%26utm_medium%3Dbanner02%26utm_content%3Dlol";
					case "unknown-3":
						return "https://play.google.com/store/apps/details?id=gg.op.lol.android&referrer=utm_source%3Dopgg%26utm_medium%3Dbanner03%26utm_content%3Dpubg";
					default:
						return "itms-apps://itunes.apple.com/kr/app/apple-store/id605722237";
				}
			};
			this.getMobileOS = function(){
				var userAgent = navigator.userAgent || navigator.vendor;

				if (/android/i.test(userAgent)) {
					return "Android";
				}

				if (/iPad|iPhone|iPod/.test(userAgent)) {
					return "iOS";
				}

				return "unknown";
			};
			this.getLang = function(){
				return document.documentElement.lang || "en";
			};

			this.slots = [
				{
					'id': '5a84644f46e0fb0001d74d3c',
					'size': '970x90'
				},
				{
					'id': '5a84640c46e0fb0001fc3bb0',
					'size': '300x250'
				},
				{
					'id': '5a8462a746e0fb0001bf35aa',
					'size': 'skyscraper'
				},
			];
			this.getCookie = function(name){
				var match = document.cookie.match(new RegExp('(^| )' + name + '=([^;]+)'));
				if (match) return match[2];
			};
			this.bindClickEvent = function(){
				$(".lifeOnwer-" + randAdIdx).click(function(evt){
					$.OP.GG.tracker.combine.sendEvent(['FB', 'Pixel'], 'Opgg', 'ClickAd', {
						Location: location_,
						subLocation: subLocation,
						BannerType: adIndex
					});
				});
			};

			this.adIndex = Math.floor(Math.random() * (this.getMobileOS() === "iOS" ? 2 : 3)) + 1;
			this.location_ = "summoner";
			this.subLocation = "summary";


			slots.forEach(function(slot){
				if (self.getMobileOS() === "unknown" && slot.size === "300x250") {
					return;
				}
				var element = document.querySelector('.vm-placement[data-id="' + slot.id + '"]');
				if (element) {
					self.showAd(element, slot.size);
				}
			});
			this.bindClickEvent();
		};
	</script>
